I‚Äôve never had anything bad here. My favorite is the seafood curry. I also enjoy the chicken katsu curry at the super spicy level.

<Rating>5</Rating>< Text>
One of the best curry joints around. There is a good variety of food available here and prompt service. You can choose the level of spice that they make your food which is nice since curry isn't curry to me without some heat. You also have a good variety of proteins from seafood, beef, chicken, and pork. They also have a good kids menu if you're bringing long the kiddos. Parking is available for free in the shopping area . I prefer this location to the one in little Tokyo.</Text>

We had my son's birthday party at the Bakersfield location. The kiddos were stoked for the Nerf Gun War. However, it was not what we expected. First off, the room was tiny. Like maybe 30' x 15'. < text>
I am from Arizona, where I regularly get treats from Bahama Buck's. I happened upon this location in HB on 11/5/17 after a trip to the grocery store. It was right before they closed, so if they didnt want to serve us, they should have said "sorry, we're closed" and I honestly wish they would have said that. The price was about a dollar more than AZ locations but we didn't care because we were excited to find that they even exist in CA. Well, as we're being rung up, the guy making our shaved ice yells to the cashier "IT'S GONNA HAVE TO BE TO-GO!" We say Yes that's fine, cuz we were planning on that anyway. Well then he brings over our order, and throws it down without looking at us or saying anything. It's a complete rip-off disappointment; completely flat cup of smashed flat shaved ice with a flat soda lid on top and an umbrella in the straw hole. I come here for the cup of shaved ice that is ALWAYS a colorful MOUNTAIN that towers about 3 or 4 inches above the rim of the cup. This kid is needs to be fired, he ripped me off and completely killed my fascination with this place.< /text>

< Text>
BMW 740 (E38, M62) is my daily driver since 1998. Nicknamed the Beast, it has been mechanically bullet-proof because it is well-maintained. However, @ 164K miles it experienced a timing chain guide failure. If you Google this mechanical issue you find a complex repair is required; between 18 and 30 hours of labor.

Faced with the choice to scrap or keep the car, I turned to the most trusted BMW service shop in the Bay area. German Motor Specialist, recently acquired by Stress-Free Auto Care, still retains it's core mechanical team and chief service advisor, Paul Pisano. All techs have BMW repair certifications & many years of experience. Shop floor is super clean & each work area is well organized!

Paul guided the repair & kept it w/in estimate! No surprises. My mechanic completed the repair using BMW OEM parts & timing was restored to spec. using precision BMW tools. In the process, the engine was nearly completely resealed.

Engine now runs & accelerates smoothly. Beast is still my ultimate driving machine & fingers crossed, could see another 100K miles.

Thanks GMS<//Text>

< Text>
3 week update:
Clean gym, staff is professional, and the app makes for a smooth experience. The app tells me how crowded the gym is so i can plan accordingly, and the people are very nice and typically mind their own workouts.
Everyone cleans after themselves and there are always plenty of cleaning supplies to ensure the gym stays that way. The lockers here are better than at other places.                          Surprisingly, the showers are still open (limited-capacity, yet I have seen other gyms keep their showers closed), and the lockers feel like a luxury given the very low membership price.
The touchless membership sign-in is also helpful and offers a smooth experience at the entrance (wouldn't mind if it remained after the pandemic ends).
Worth the price.</Text>

<userid>118255687420082471679<//userid><Name>Jason Moreno<//Name><time>1618878854414< /time>< Rate>

<Text>Buffalo Wild Wings is always a solid choice.

We stopped in to get some wings, beer, and watch the Oakland A's crush the Detroit Tigers.

They were working with an understandable limited menu.  Didn't matter because then stuff that wasn't being served wasn't on our radar.

We ordered small fries, small onion rings, 20 traditional wings and we both had a few big IPAs.
We went with 3 flavors, Asian Zing, Spicy Garlic, and traditional Hot.

Everything was cooked well and served hot and fresh.  The three sauces were very tasty and the wings came with celery, carrots, and both blues cheese and ranch dressing on the side.

It also looked as if there were limited taps but seemed as if they still had a good variety available.

Our server was the bartender and he was great!  Very attentive and brought our food quickly and had fresh beers every time we got low.

The only drawback is that they don't offer the trivia boxes because of COVID.  It's somewhat understandable but a year into it now, we should be able to get the boxes with a quick wipe of sanitizer from the server.  It wouldn't take very long to do for each box and sure wouldn't add anything to the bottom line as I'm sure they have some kind of sanitizer on hand already.

Again, this is a great spot and I do encourage you to go.  There weren't many people when I was there and I'm sure not only could the restaurant use your business but so could the servers and bartenders.

Go... Enjoy... and tip well...

If you like my reviews, hit the "Thumbs Up"!!

Wanna see more places that I go, things that I eat, and stuff that I do??
Then...

< review>
First time eating here, service was okay. We arrived about 430pm, not too busy, by the time we left about 545pm it was pretty busy.We ordered the traditional and boneless combo with boneless Caribbean jerk and traditional wings in Thai curry. It took about 30 mins to get the order on the table and when it finally came it was mediocre. There was a very small amount of coleslaw and fries. It's obvious this combo is made for one person, my husband and I decided to share it. It was $18.99, which in my opinion is a little steep for the amount of food that was on the plate but there is essentially enough food in this combo for one person to enjoy. Price point is still high if that's the case. The Caribbean jerk flavor was not as good. It had this distinct, hard to explain taste to it, perhaps it was one of the spices used? Thai curry is pretty spicy but has a really good flavor that I continued to crave after we left. That's the only reason I gave this 3 stars, not  sure if this is enough to bring us back here.< /review>

<userid>113454952818054781481< /userid>< text>
Interesting place. We arrived and the guy at the door said "Oh, I don't know if we have any tables available"... we look inside, and half the restaurant is empty. We look confused. He says he'll go try and find one. He finds one! We are seated. We get our menus. The alcohol menu (beer, wine and cocktails) do not have ANY prices on them, just calories. Again, we are confused. We ask our waiter why there are no prices on the drink menu, he goes and checks. Comes back, says he can go and find out the prices of whatever drinks we want. <review>Horribly managed.  We had a booth near the entrance and could hear everything.  Every customer that came in was greeted with an apology.  They've apologized so much, it's habitual!  Each new customer was told that no booth was available.  There were at least a half-dozen empty booths with dirty dishes sitting on them the entire 2+ hours we were there.  One group of customers, seated outside, marched back out after waiting 30+ minutes for someone to come by.

Our experience fit the same picture.  I ordered a beer immediately and didn't get it for at least a half hour, after our food came!  Most of the time we were there, my glass was empty.  Not one dirty dish or glass was carried away during the entire 2+ hours.

On top of that, this location has really high prices.  A medium order of wings is $19.49.  Fries, potato wedges, and drinks are not included.

There is something wrong with Buffalo Wild Wings.  This location has below average service for the chain, and BWW as a whole has well below average service.  As much as I love Asian zing wings and potato wedges with ranch, I just can't justify going any more.<//review>< pictures>
